NodeStatus {\n55\t    /// Check if a transition from `self` to `new_status` is valid.\n56\t    ///\n57\t    /// # State Transition Rules\n58\t    ///\n59\t    /// | From | To | Triggered by |\n60\t    /// |------|-----|-------------|\n61\t    /// | (new) | Joining | `POST /_miroir/nodes` |\n62\t    /// | Joining | Active | Migration complete |\n63\t    /// | Active | Draining | `POST /_miroir/nodes/{id}/drain` |\n64\t    /// | Draining | Removed | Migration complete |\n65\t    /// | Active/Draining | Failed | Health check detects |\n66\t    /// | Failed | Active | Health check {\n70\t        match (self, new_status) {\n71\t            // Initial state\n72\t            (NodeStatus::Joining, NodeStatus::Active) => true,\n73\t\n74\t            // Normal operations\n75\t            (NodeStatus::Active, NodeStatus::Draining) => true,\n76\t            (NodeStatus::Draining, NodeStatus::Removed) => true,\n77\t\n78\t            // Failure and recovery\n79\t            (NodeStatus::Active, NodeStatus::Failed) => true,\n80\t            (NodeStatus::Draining, NodeStatus::Failed) => true,\n81\t            (NodeStatus::Failed, NodeStatus::Active) => true,\n82\t\n83\t            // Degradation\n84\t            (NodeStatus::Active, NodeStatus::Degraded) => true,\n85\t            (NodeStatus::Failed, NodeStatus::Degraded) => true,\n86\t            (NodeStatus::Degraded, (NodeStatus::Active, NodeStatus::Healthy) => true,\n91\t\n92\t            // Same state is always valid\n93\t            (s, t) if s == t => true,\n94\t\n95\t            // All other transitions are |--------|----------------|-------|\n108\t    /// | Healthy/Active | Yes | Normal operation |\n109\t    /// | Degraded | Yes | Partial failures, still accepting writes |\n110\t    /// | Joining | No |   NodeStatus::Joining | NodeStatus::Failed | NodeStatus::Removed => false,\n123\t            NodeStatus::Draining => !draining_shard.is_some(),\n124\t        }\n125\t    }\n126\t}\n127\t\n128\timpl         NodeStatus::Degraded => write!(f, \"degraded\"),\n133\t            NodeStatus::Active => write!(f, \"active\"),\n134\t            NodeStatus::Joining => write!(f, \"joining\"),\n135\t            NodeStatus::Draining => write!(f, \"draining\"),\n136\t            NodeStatus::Failed => write!(f, \"failed\"),\n137\t            NodeStatus::Removed => write!(f, \"removed\"),\n138\t        }\n139\t    }\n140\t}\n141\t\n142\t/// A single Meilisearch node in the topology.\n143\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n144\tpub struct Node {\n145\t    /// Unique node {"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"call_ade3a7890d9d47e9b51ead0a","type":"tool_result","content":"1\t//! Rendezvous hash-based routing and shard assignment.\n2\t\n3\tuse crate::topology::{Group, NodeId, Topology};\n4\tuse std::hash::{Hash, Hasher};\n5\tuse twox_hash::XxHash64;\n6\t\n7\t/// Compute a rendezvous score for a shard+node pair.\n8\t///\n9\t/// Higher scores win; used for deterministic shard assignment.\n10\t///\n11\t/// CRITICAL: Uses seed 0 to match Meilisearch Enterprise's hash function.\n12\t/// Any deviation (different seed, different ordering, endianness) forks\n13\t/// routing across any two Miroir instances and silently corrupts writes.\n14\tpub fn score(shard_id: u32, node_id: &str) -> u64 {\n15\t    let mut h = XxHash64::with_seed(0);\n16\t    shard_id.hash(&mut h);\n17\t    node_id.hash(&mut h);\n18\t    h.finish()\n19\t}\n20\t\n21\t/// Assign a shard to `rf` nodes within a single replica group.\n22\t///\n23\t/// `group_nodes` is the subset of nodes belonging to that group.\n24\t///\n25\t/// Nodes are sorted by score descending, with ties broken lexicographically\n26\t/// by node_id to ensure deterministic assignment even when hash scores collide.\n27\tpub fn assign_shard_in_group(shard_id: u32, group_nodes: &[NodeId], rf: usize) -> Vec<NodeId> {\n28\t    let mut scored: Vec<(u64, &NodeId)> = group_nodes\n29\t        .iter()\n30\t        .map(|n| (score(shard_id, n.as_str()), n))\n31\t        .collect();\n32\t    scored.sort_unstable_by(|a, b| {\n33\t        b.0.cmp(&a.0)\n34\t            .then_with(|| a.1.as_str().cmp(b.1.as_str()))\n35\t    });\n36\t    scored\n37\t        .into_iter()\n38\t        .take(rf)\n39\t        .map(|(_, n)| n.clone())\n40\t        .collect()\n41\t}\n42\t\n43\t/// All write targets for a document: the RF nodes in EACH replica group.\n44\tpub fn write_targets(shard_id: u32, topology: &Topology) -> Vec<NodeId> {\n45\t    topology\n46\t        .groups()\n47\t        .flat_map(|group| assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, group.nodes(), topology.rf()))\n48\t        .collect()\n49\t}\n50\t\n51\t/// Select the replica group for a query (round-robin by query counter).\n52\tpub fn query_group(query_seq: u64, replica_groups: u32) -> u32 {\n53\t    (query_seq % replica_groups as u64) as u32\n54\t}\n55\t\n56\t/// The covering set for a search: one node per shard within the chosen group.\n57\t///\n58\t/// Returns a Vec where index i contains the node to query for shard i.\n59\t/// The length is always exactly shard_count, even if multiple shards\n60\t/// map to the same node.\n61\tpub fn covering_set(shard_count: u32, group: &Group, rf: usize, query_seq: u64) -> Vec<NodeId> {\n62\t    (0..shard_count)\n63\t        .map(|shard_id| {\n64\t            let replicas = assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, group.nodes(), rf);\n65\t            // rotate through replicas for intra-group load balancing\n66\t            replicas[(query_seq as usize) % replicas.len()].clone()\n67\t        })\n68\t        .collect()\n69\t}\n70\t\n71\t/// Compute the shard ID for a document's primary key.\n72\tpub fn shard_for_key(primary_key: &str, shard_count: u32) -> u32 {\n73\t    let mut h = XxHash64::with_seed(0);\n74\t    primary_key.hash(&mut h);\n75\t    (h.finish() % shard_count as u64) as u32\n76\t}\n77\t\n78\t#[cfg(test)]\n79\tmod tests {\n80\t    use super::*;\n81\t    use crate::topology::{Node, NodeId};\n82\t\n83\t    // Test 1: Rendezvous assignment is deterministic given fixed node list\n84\t    #[test]\n85\t    fn test_rendezvous_determinism() {\n86\t        let nodes: Vec<NodeId> = vec![\"node1\", \"node2\", \"node3\"]\n87\t            .into_iter()\n88\t            .map(|s| NodeId::new(s.to_string()))\n89\t            .collect();\n90\t        let shard_id = 42;\n91\t\n92\t        let assignment1 = assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, across calls\n99\t    #[test]\n100\t    fn test_score_stability() {\n101\t        let score1 = score(123, \"node1\");\n102\t        let score2 = score(123, \"node1\");\n103\t        assert_eq!(score1, score2);\n104\t    }\n105\t\n106\t    // Test 3: Different shard+node pairs produce different scores\n107\t    #[test]\n108\t    fn test_score_uniqueness() {\n109\t        let score1 = score(1, \"node1\");\n110\t        let score2 = score(1, \"node2\");\n111\t        let score3 = score(2, \"node1\");\n112\t\n113\t        assert_ne!(score1, score2);\n114\t        assert_ne!(score1, score3);\n115\t        assert_ne!(score2, score3);\n116\t    }\n117\t\n118\t    // Test 4: Adding a 4th node moves at most ~2 × (1/4) of shards\n119\t    #[test]\n120\t    fn test_minimal_reshuffling_on_add() {\n121\t        let nodes_3: Vec<NodeId> = vec![\"node1\", \"node2\", \"node3\"]\n122\t            .into_iter()\n123\t            .map(|s| NodeId::new(s.to_string()))\n124\t            .collect();\n125\t        let nodes_4: Vec<NodeId> = vec![\"node1\", \"node2\", \"node3\", \"node4\"]\n126\t            .into_iter()\n127\t            .map(|s| NodeId::new(s.to_string()))\n128\t            .collect();\n129\t\n130\t        let shard_count = 100;\n131\t        let rf = 1;\n132\t\n133\t        let mut moved_count = 0;\n134\t        for        }\n143\t\n144\t        // Expected: at most ~2 × (1/4) = 50% of shards\n145\t        let max_expected = (shard_count as f64 * 0.5).ceil() as usize;\n146\t        assert!(\n147\t .into_iter()\n157\t            .map(|s| NodeId::new(s.to_string()))\n158\t            .collect();\n159\t        let shard_count = 64;\n160\t        let rf = 1;\n161\t\n162\t        let mut eprintln!(\"Actual shard distribution: {node_shard_counts:?}\");\n176\t\n177\t        // DoD requirement: each node holds 15–27 shards\n178\t        // This accommodates natural variance in hash-based assert_eq!(total, shard_count as usize);\n189\t    }\n190\t\n191\t    // Test 6: Top-RF placement changes minimally on add/remove\n192\t    #[test]\n193\t    fn test_top_rf_stability() {\n194\t        let nodes_3: Vec<NodeId> = vec![\"node1\", \"node2\", \"node3\"]\n195\t            .into_iter()\n196\t            .map(|s| NodeId::new(s.to_string()))\n197\t            .collect();\n198\t        let nodes_4: Vec<NodeId> = vec![\"node1\", \"node2\", \"node3\", \"node4\"]\n199\t            .into_iter()\n200\t            .map(|s| NodeId::new(s.to_string()))\n201\t            .collect();\n202\t        let rf = 2;\n203\t        let shard_count = 100;\n204\t\n205\t        let mut changed_count = 0;\n206\t        for shard_id in 0..shard_count {\n207\t            let assign_3 =       // A change is if the intersection is less than RF\n215\t            let intersection = set_3.intersection(&set_4).count();\n216\t            if intersection < rf {\n217\t                changed_count += 1;\n218\t            }\n219\t        }\n220\t\n221\t        // Adding a 4th node affects approximately 1/4 of assignments\n222\t        // But with RF=2, we need to account for overlap\n223\t        // Expected: roughly 50-60% might have some change\n224\t        let max_expected = (shard_count as f64 * 0.6).ceil() as usize;\n225\t        assert!(\n226\t            changed_count <= max_expected,\n227\t            \"Expected ≤ {max_expected} shards to change, but {changed_count} changed\"\n228\t        );\n229\t\n230\t        // Also verify that not everything {min_expected} shards to change, but only {changed_count} changed\"\n235\t        );\n236\t    }\n237\t\n238\t    // Test 7: write_targets returns exactly RG × RF nodes\n239\t    #[test]\n240\t    fn );\n351\t            topology.add_node(node);\n352\t        }\n353\t\n354\t        let group = topology.group(group_id).unwrap();\n355\t        let shard_count = 10;\n356\t        let rf =  .into_iter()\n543\t            .map(|s| NodeId::new(s.to_string()))\n544\t            .collect();\n545\t\n546\t        for run in 0..1000 {\n547\t            let shard_id = (run % 100) as u32; // → at most 2 × (1/4) × 64 edges differ\n562\t    #[test]\n563\t    fn acceptance_reshuffle_bound_on_add() {\n564\t        let nodes_3: Vec<NodeId> = vec![\"node1\", \"node2\", \"node3\"]\n565\t            .into_iter()\n566\t            .map(|s| NodeId::new(s.to_string()))\n567\t            .collect();\n568\t        let nodes_4: Vec<NodeId> = vec![\"node1\", \"node2\", \"node3\", \"node4\"]\n569\t            .into_iter()\n570\t            .map(|s| NodeId::new(s.to_string()))\n571\t            .collect();\n572\t\n573\t        let shard_count = 64;\n574\t        let rf = 1;\n575\t\n576\t        let mut moved_count = 0;\n577\t        for shard_id in 0..shard_count {\n578\t            let assign_3 = assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, &nodes_3, rf);\n579\t            let assign_4 = assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, &nodes_4, rf);\n580\t\n581\t            // Shard moved if its primary owner changed\n582\t            if assign_3.first() != assign_4.first() {\n583\t                moved_count += 1;\n584\t            }\n585\t        }\n586\t\n587\t        // Expected: at most 2 × (1/4) × 64 = 32 edges differ\n588\t        let max_expected = (2.0 * (1.0 / 4.0) * shard_count as differed\"\n592\t        );\n593\t    }\n594\t\n595\t    // AT-3: Reshuffle bound on remove: 64 shards, 4→3 nodes → ~RF × S / Ng edges differ\n596\t    #[test]\n597\t    fn acceptance_reshuffle_bound_on_remove() {\n598\t        let nodes_4: Vec<NodeId> = vec![\"node1\", \"node2\", \"node3\", \"node4\"]\n599\t            .into_iter()\n600\t            .map(|s| NodeId::new(s.to_string()))\n601\t            .collect();\n602\t        let nodes_3: Vec<NodeId> = vec![\"node1\", \"node2\", \"node3\"]\n603\t            .into_iter()\n604\t            .map(|s| NodeId::new(s.to_string()))\n605\t            .collect();\n606\t\n607\t        let shard_count = 64;\n608\t        let rf = 2;\n609\t\n610\t        let mut moved_count = 0;\n611\t        for shard_id in 0..shard_count {\n612\t            let assign_4 = assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, &nodes_4, rf);\n613\t            let assign_3 = assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, &nodes_3, rf);\n614\t\n615\t            // Count edges that differ\n616\t            let set_4: std::collections::HashSet<_> = assign_4.iter().collect();\n617\t            let set_3: std::collections::HashSet<_> = assign_3.iter().collect();\n618\t\n619\t            // An edge differs if it's not in both sets\n620\t            let diff = set_4.symmetric_difference(&set_3).count();\n621\t            if diff > 0 {\n622\t                moved_count += diff;\n623\t            }\n624\t        }\n625\t\n626\t        // Expected: ~RF × S / Ng = 2 × 64 / 4 = 32 edges differ\n627\t        // Allow some variance due to hash distribution\n628\t        let expected = (rf * shard_count as usize) / 4;\n629\t        let tolerance = (expected as f64 * 0.9).ceil() as usize; // ±90%\n630\t        assert!(\n631\t            moved_count >= expected - tolerance && moved_count <= expected + tolerance,\n632\t            \"Expected ~{expected} shard-node edges to differ (±{tolerance}), but {moved_count} differed\"\n633\t        );\n634\t    }\n635\t\n636\t    // AT-4: Uniformity: 64 shards, 3 nodes, RF=1 → each node holds 18–26 shards\n637\t    #[test]\n638\t    fn acceptance_uniformity_64_shards_3_nodes_rf1() {\n639\t        let nodes: Vec<NodeId> = vec![\"node1\", \"node2\", \"node3\"]\n640\t            .into_iter()\n641\t            .map(|s| NodeId::new(s.to_string()))\n642\t            .collect();\n643\t        let shard_count = 64;\n644\t        let rf = 1;\n645\t\n646\t        let mut node_shard_counts: std::collections::HashMap<String, usize> =\n647\t            std::collections::HashMap::new();\n648\t\n649\t        for shard_id in 0..shard_count {\n650\t            let assignment = assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, &nodes, rf);\n651\t            if let }\n656\t        }\n657\t\n658\t        // DoD requirement: each node holds 15–27 shards\n659\t        for (node, count) in &node_shard_counts {\n660\t            assert!(\n661\t                *count node is added or removed\n672\t    #[test]\n673\t    fn acceptance_rf2_placement_stability() {\n674\t        let nodes_3: Vec<NodeId> = vec![\"node1\", \"node2\", \"node3\"]\n675\t            .into_iter()\n676\t            .map(|s| NodeId::new(s.to_string()))\n677\t            .collect();\n678\t        let nodes_4: Vec<NodeId> = vec![\"node1\", \"node2\", \"node3\", \"node4\"]\n679\t            .into_iter()\n680\t            .map(|s| NodeId::new(s.to_string()))\n681\t            .collect();\n682\t\n683\t        let shard_count = 64;\n684\t        let rf = 2;\n685\t\n686\t        let mut \"/synonyms\",\n55\t            axum::routing::get(get_synonyms).put(update_synonyms).delete(delete_synonyms),\n56\t        )\n57\t        .route(\n58\t            \"/distinct-attribute\",\n59\t            axum::routing::get(get_distinct_attribute).put(update_distinct_attribute).delete(delete_distinct_attribute),\n60\t        )\n61\t        .route(\n62\t            \"/typo-tolerance\",\n63\t            axum::routing::get(get_typo_tolerance).put(update_typo_tolerance).delete(delete_typo_tolerance),\n64\t        )\n65\t        .route(\n66\t            \"/faceting\",\n67\t            axum::routing::get(get_faceting).put(update_faceting).delete(delete_faceting),\n68\t        )\n69\t        .route(\n70\t            \"/pagination\",\n71\t            axum::routing::get(get_pagination).put(update_pagination).delete(delete_pagination),\n72\t        )\n73\t}\n74\t\n75\t/// GET /indexes/:index/settings - Get all settings.\n76\tasync fn get_all_settings(\n77\t    State(state): State<ProxyState>,\n78\t    Path(index): Path<String>,\n79\t) -> Result<Json<Value>, ErrorResponse> {\n80\t    let topology = state.topology().await;\n81\t\n82\t    // Query first available node\n83\t    for group in topology.groups() {\n84\t        if let Some(node_id) = group.nodes().first() {\n85\t            let request = ScatterRequest {\n86\t                method: \"GET\".to_string(),\n87\t                path: format!(\"/indexes/{}/settings\", index),\n88\t                body: vec![],\n89\t                headers: vec![],\n90\t            };\n91\t\n92\t            let scatter = HttpScatter::new((*state.client).clone(), state.config.server.request_timeout_ms);\n93\t\n94\t            let result = scatter\n95\t                .scatter(&topology, vec![node_id.clone()], request, UnavailableShardPolicy::Partial)\n96\t                .await\n97\t                .map_err(|e| ErrorResponse::internal_error(e.to_string()))?;\n98\t\n99\t            if let Some(resp) = result.responses.first() {\n100\t                if resp.status == 200 {\n101\t                    let body: Value = serde_json::from_slice(&resp.body)\n102\t                        .unwrap_or_else(|_| Value::Null);\n103\t                    return Ok(Json(body));\n104\t                } else if resp.status == 404 {\n105\t                    return Err(ErrorResponse::index_not_found(&index));\n106\t                }\n107\t            }\n108\t        }\n109\t    }\n110\t\n111\t    Err(ErrorResponse::index_not_found(&index))\n112\t}\n113\t\n114\t/// Cached original value for rollback.\n115\tstruct RollbackValue {\n116\t    /// The original value to restore on rollback.\n117\t    original_value: Option<Value>,\n118\t    /// Whether the setting existed before.\n119\t    existed: bool,\n120\t}\n121\t\n122\t/// Generic handler for updating a setting with rollback.\n123\tasync fn update_setting_with_rollback(\n124\t    state: &ProxyState,\n125\t    index: &str,\n126\t    setting_path: &str,\n127\t    value: &Value,\n128\t) -> Result<Response, ErrorResponse> {\n129\t    let topology = state.topology().await;\n130\t    let targets = write_targets(0, &topology);\n131\t\n132\t    if targets.is_empty() {\n133\t        return Err(ErrorResponse::internal_error(\"No nodes available\"));\n134\t    }\n135\t\n136\t    // Step 1: Fetch current values from all nodes for rollback\n137\t    let mut rollback_values: std::collections::HashMap<String, RollbackValue> = std::collections::HashMap::new();\n138\t\n139\t    for target in &targets {\n140\t        let get_request = ScatterRequest {\n141\t            method: \"GET\".to_string(),\n142\t            path: format!(\"/indexes/{}/{}\", index, setting_path),\n143\t            body: vec![],\n144\t            headers: vec![],\n145\t        };\n146\t\n147\t        let scatter = HttpScatter::new((*state.client).clone(), state.config.server.request_timeout_ms);\n148\t\n149\t        match scatter.scatter(&topology, vec![target.clone()], get_request, UnavailableShardPolicy::Partial).await {\n150\t            Ok(resp) => {\n151\t                if let Some(r) = resp.responses.first() {\n152\t                    let original_value = if r.status == 200 {\n153\t                        Some(serde_json::from_slice(&r.body).unwrap_or(Value::Null))\n154\t                    } else {\n155\t                        None\n156\t                    };\n157\t                    rollback_values.insert(\n158\t                        target.as_str().to_string(),\n159\t                        RollbackValue {\n160\t                            original_value,\n161\t                            existed: r.status == 200,\n162\t                        },\n163\t                    );\n164\t                }\n165\t            }\n166\t            Err(_) => {\n167\t                // Node is already down, skip rollback for it\n168\t                rollback_values.insert(target.as_str().to_string(), RollbackValue {\n169\t                    original_value: None,\n170\t                    existed: false,\n171\t                });\n172\t            }\n173\t        }\n174\t    }\n175\t\n176\t    let body_bytes = serde_json::to_vec(value).unwrap_or_default();\n177\t\n178\t    let request = ScatterRequest {\n179\t        method: \"PUT\".to_string(),\n180\t        path: format!(\"/indexes/{}/{}\", index, setting_path),\n181\t        body: body_bytes,\n182\t        headers: vec![],\n183\t    };\n184\t\n185\t    let scatter = HttpScatter::new((*state.client).clone(), state.config.server.request_timeout_ms);\n186\t\n187\t    // Track successful nodes for rollback\n188\t    let mut successful_nodes: Vec<String> = Vec::new();\n189\t    let mut last_response: Option<Value> = None;\n190\t\n191\t    // Sequential broadcast with rollback on failure\n192\t    for target in &targets {\n193\t        let result = scatter\n194\t            .scatter(&topology, vec![target.clone()], request.clone(), UnavailableShardPolicy::Error)\n195\t            .await;\n196\t\n197\t        match result {\n198\t            Ok(resp) => {\n199\t                if let Some(r) = resp.responses.first() {\n200\t                    if (200..300).contains(&r.status) {\n201\t                        successful_nodes.push(target.as_str().to_string());\n202\t                        let body: Value = serde_json::from_slice(&r.body).unwrap_or(Value::Null);\n203\t                        last_response = Some(body);\n204\t                    } else {\n205\t                        // Rollback from successful nodes\n206\t                        rollback_setting(state, &topology, &successful_nodes, &rollback_values, index, setting_path).await;\n207\t                        return Err(ErrorResponse::internal_error(format!(\n208\t                            \"Failed to update setting on node {}: status {}\",\n209\t                            target.as_str(),\n210\t                            r.status\n211\t                        )));\n212\t                    }\n213\t                }\n214\t            }\n215\t            Err(e) => {\n216\t                // Rollback from successful nodes\n217\t                rollback_setting(state, &topology, &successful_nodes, &rollback_values, index, setting_path).await;\n218\t                return Err(ErrorResponse::internal_error(format!(\n219\t                    \"Failed to update setting on node {}: {}\",\n220\t                    target.as_str(),\n221\t                    e\n222\t                )));\n223\t            }\n224\t        }\n225\t    }\n226\t\n227\t    let response_body = if let Some(body) = last_response {\n228\t        body\n229\t    } else {\n230\t        let task_uid = state.task_manager.next_uid();\n231\t        serde_json::json!({\n232\t            \"taskUid\": task_uid,\n233\t            \"indexUid\": index,\n234\t            \"status\": \"enqueued\",\n235\t            \"type\": \"settingsUpdate\",\n236\t            \"enqueuedAt\": chrono::Utc::now().to_rfc3339(),\n237\t        })\n238\t    };\n239\t\n240\t    Ok((axum::http::StatusCode::ACCEPTED, Json(response_body)).into_response())\n241\t}\n242\t\n243\t/// Rollback a setting from nodes that were successfully updated.\n244\tasync fn rollback_setting(\n245\t    state: &ProxyState,\n246\t    topology: &miroir_core::topology::Topology,\n247\t    successful_nodes: &[String],\n248\t    rollback_values: &std::collections::HashMap<String, RollbackValue>,\n249\t    index: &str,\n250\t    setting_path: &str,\n251\t) {\n252\t    for node_id in successful_nodes {\n253\t        if let Some(rollback) = rollback_values.get(node_id) {\n254\t            let node_id_ref = miroir_core::topology::NodeId::new(node_id.clone());\n255\t            if rollback.existed {\n256\t                // Restore original value\n257\t                if let Some(original) = &rollback.original_value {\n258\t                    let body_bytes = serde_json::to_vec(original).unwrap_or_default();\n259\t                    let _ = state\n260\t                        .client\n261\t                        .send_to_node(\n262\t                            topology,\n263\t                            &node_id_ref,\n264\t                            \"PUT\",\n265\t                            &format!(\"/indexes/{}/{}\", index, setting_path),\n266\t                            Some(&body_bytes),\n267\t                            &[],\n268\t                        )\n269\t                        .await;\n270\t                }\n271\t            } else {\n272\t                // Setting didn't exist before, delete it\n273\t                let _ = state\n274\t                    .client\n275\t                    .send_to_node(\n276\t                        topology,\n277\t                        &node_id_ref,\n278\t                        \"DELETE\",\n279\t                        &format!(\"/indexes/{}/{}\", index, setting_path),\n280\t                        None,\n281\t                        &[],\n282\t                    )\n283\t                    .await;\n284\t            }\n285\t        }\n286\t    }\n287\t}\n288\t\n289\t/// GET /indexes/:index/settings/filterable-attributes\n290\tasync fn get_filterable_attributes(\n291\t    State(state): State<ProxyState>,\n292\t    Path(index): Path<String>,\n293\t) -> Result<Json<Value>, ErrorResponse> {\n294\t    get_setting(&state, &index, \"filterable-attributes\").await\n295\t}\n296\t\n297\t/// Json<Value>,\n302\t) -> Result<Response, ErrorResponse> {\n303\t    // Ensure _miroir_shard is always in filterable attributes\n304\t    let mut updated = body.0.clone();\n305\t    if let Some(arr) = {\n570\t    delete_setting(&state, &index, \"settings/pagination\").await\n571\t}\n572\t\n573\t/// Generic GET handler for a setting.\n574\tasync fn get_setting(\n575\t    state: &ProxyState,\n576\t    index: &str,\n577\t    setting_path: &str,\n578\t) -> Result<Json<Value>, ErrorResponse> {\n579\t    let topology = state.topology().await;\n580\t\n581\t    for group in topology.groups() {\n582\t        if let Some(node_id) = group.nodes().first() {\n583\t            let request = ScatterRequest {\n584\t                method: \"GET\".to_string(),\n585\t                path: format!(\"/indexes/{}/{}\", index, setting_path),\n586\t                body: vec![],\n587\t                headers: vec![],\n588\t            };\n589\t\n590\t            let scatter = HttpScatter::new((*state.client).clone(), state.config.server.request_timeout_ms);\n591\t\n592\t            let result = scatter\n593\t                .scatter(&topology, vec![node_id.clone()], request, UnavailableShardPolicy::Partial)\n594\t                .await\n595\t                .map_err(|e| ErrorResponse::internal_error(e.to_string()))?;\n596\t\n597\t            if let Some(resp) = result.responses.first() {\n598\t                if resp.status == 200 {\n599\t                    let value: Value = serde_json::from_slice(&resp.body)\n600\t                        .map_err(|_| ErrorResponse::internal_error(\"Invalid JSON response\"))?;\n601\t                    return Ok(Json(value));\n602\t                } else if resp.status == 404 {\n603\t                    return Err(ErrorResponse::index_not_found(index));\n604\t                }\n605\t            }\n606\t        }\n607\t    }\n608\t\n609\t    Err(ErrorResponse::index_not_found(index))\n610\t}\n611\t\n612\t/// the actual routing code to compute shard assignments and estimate\n253\t/// storage/write load. Document keys are synthesized for the corpus size\n254\t/// and routed through the real hash function to measure distribution.\n255\tpub fn simulate(params: &SimParams) -> SimResult {\n256\t    let total_docs = params.corpus_size_bytes / params.doc_size_bytes;\n257\t    let rf = params.replication_factor;\n258\t    let rg = params.replica_groups;\n259\t    let nodes_per_group = })\n270\t        .collect();\n271\t\n272\t    // Simulate document distribution across old and new shard counts.\n273\t    // Use the actual router hash to get realistic distribution.\n274\t    let mut old_shard_counts: Vec<u64> = vec![0; params.old_shards as usize];\n275\t    let mut new_shard_counts: Vec<u64> = vec![0; params.new_shards as usize];\n276\t\n277\t    // Track per-node storage for old and new shard assignments.\n278\t    // Each group stores the full corpus; each node in a group stores its\n279\t    // rendezvous-assigned fraction.\n280\t    let total_nodes = (rg as usize) * nodes_per_group;\n281\t    let mut node_storage_old: Vec<u64> = vec![0; total_nodes];\n282\t    let mut node_storage_new: Vec<u64> = vec![0; total_nodes];\n283\t\n284\t    for i in 0..total_docs {\n285\t        let key = format!(\"doc-{i}\");\n286\t        let old_shard = shard_for_key(&key, params.old_shards);\n287\t        let new_shard = shard_for_key(&key, params.new_shards);\n288\t\n289\t        old_shard_counts[old_shard as usize] += 1;\n290\t        new_shard_counts[new_shard as usize] += 1;\n291\t\n292\t        // For each replica group, assign shard to RF nodes.\n293\t        for (g_idx, group) in groups.iter().enumerate() {\n294\t            let old_targets = assign_shard_in_group(old_shard, group.nodes(), rf);\n295\t            let new_targets = assign_shard_in_group(new_shard, group.nodes(), rf);\n296\t\n297\t            for node_id in &old_targets {\n298\t                let node_idx = g_idx * nodes_per_group\n299\t                    + group.nodes().iter().position(|n| n == node_id).unwrap_or(0);\n300\t                node_storage_old[node_idx] += params.doc_size_bytes;\n301\t            }\n302\t            for node_id in &new_targets {\n303\t                let node_idx = g_idx * nodes_per_group\n304\t                    + group.nodes().iter().position(|n| n == node_id).unwrap_or(0);\n305\t                node_storage_new[node_idx] += params.doc_size_bytes;\n306\t            }\n307\t        }\n308\t    }\n309\t\n310\t    // Compute distribution coefficients of variation.\n311\t    let old_cv = cv(&old_shard_counts);\n312\t    let new_cv = cv(&new_shard_counts);\n313\t\n314\t    // Normal storage: corpus replicated across RG groups.\n315\t    let normal_storage_bytes = params.corpus_size_bytes * rg as u64;\n316\t    // Peak storage: live + shadow (both fully populated).\n317\t    let peak_storage_bytes = normal_storage_bytes * 2;\n318\t\n319\t    // Per-node storage (max across all nodes).\n320\t    let per_node_normal = node_storage_old.iter().copied().max().unwrap_or(0);\n321\t    let per_node_peak = per_node_normal + node_storage_new.iter().copied().max().unwrap_or(0);\n322\t\n323\t    // Write rates.\n324\t    // Normal: each incoming doc → RF × RG actual node writes.\n325\t    let normal_write_rate = params.write_rate_dps * rf as u64 * rg as u64;\n326\t    // Dual-write: each incoming doc → 2 × (RF × RG) writes (old + new assignment).\n327\t    let dual_write_rate = normal_write_rate * 2;\n328\t    // Backfill: reads all docs, writes each to new assignment → RF × RG writes/doc.\n329\t    // Plus ongoing dual-writes for new incoming docs.\n330\t    let backfill_write_rate = params.backfill_throttle_dps * rf as u64 * rg as u64;\n331\t    let peak_write_rate = dual_write_rate + backfill_write_rate;\n332\t\n333\t    let dual_write_amplification = 2.0;\n334\t    let peak_write_amplification = peak_write_rate as f64 / normal_write_rate as f64;\n335\t\n336\t    // Backfill duration: total docs / throttle rate.\n337\t    let backfill_duration_secs = if params.backfill_throttle_dps > 0 {\n338\t        total_docs as f64 / params.backfill_throttle_dps as f64\n339\t    } else {\n340\t        f64::INFINITY\n341\t    };\n342\t\n343\t    // Total bytes written during reshard:\n344\t    // 1. Dual-write ongoing for the full reshard duration.\n345\t    // 2. Backfill writes of entire corpus.\n346\t    // Approximate: backfill_duration × dual_write_rate + corpus × RF × RG.\n347\t    let total_reshard_write_bytes = if params.backfill_throttle_dps > 0 {\n348\t        let dual_write_bytes =\n349\t            backfill_duration_secs * dual_write_rate as f64 * params.doc_size_bytes as f64;\n350\t        let backfill_bytes = total_docs * rf as u64 * rg as u64 * params.doc_size_bytes;\n351\t        (dual_write_bytes as u64) + backfill_bytes\n352\t    } else {\n353\t        0\n354\t    };\n355\t\n356\t    let storage_amplification = peak_storage_bytes as f64 / normal_storage_bytes as f64;\n357\t\n358\t    SimResult {\n359\t        label: format!(\n360\t            \"{}KB/{}GB/RG{}/RF{}\",\n361\t            params.doc_size_bytes / 1024,\n362\t            params.corpus_size_bytes / (1024 * 1024 * 1024),\n363\t            rg,\n364\t            rf\n365\t        ),\n366\t        doc_size_bytes: params.doc_size_bytes,\n367\t        corpus_size_bytes: params.corpus_size_bytes,\n368\t        total_docs,\n369\t        replica_groups: rg,\n370\t        replication_factor: rf,\n371\t        old_shards: params.old_shards,\n372\t        new_shards: params.new_shards,\n373\t        nodes_per_group,\n374\t        write_rate_dps: params.write_rate_dps,\n375\t\n376\t        normal_storage_bytes,\n377\t        peak_storage_bytes,\n378\t        storage_amplification,\n379\t\n380\t        normal_write_rate,\n381\t        dual_write_rate,\n382\t        peak_write_rate,\n383\t        dual_write_amplification,\n384\t        peak_write_amplification,\n385\t\n386\t        backfill_duration_secs,\n387\t        total_bytes_written: total_reshard_write_bytes,\n388\t\n389\t        per_node_peak_storage_bytes: per_node_peak,\n390\t        per_node_normal_storage_bytes: per_node_normal,\n391\t\n392\t        old_shard_cv: old_cv,\n393\t        new_shard_cv: new_cv,\n394\t    }\n395\t}\n396\t\n397\t/// Coefficient of variation for a distribution.\n398\tfn cv(values: &[u64]) -> f64 {\n399\t    if values.is_empty() {\n400\t        return 0.0;\n401\t    }\n402\t    let n = values.len() as f64;\n403\t    let mean = values.iter().sum::<u64>() as f64 / n;\n404\t    if mean == 0.0 {\n405\t        return 0.0;\n406\t    }\n407\t    let variance = values\n408\t        .iter()\n409\t        .map(|v| (*v as f64 - mean).powi(2))\n410\t        .sum::<f64>()\n411\t        / n;\n412\t    variance.sqrt() / mean\n413\t}\n414\t\n415\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n416\t// Tests\n417\t// {"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"call_09febe7cf8cb4fbc88b91fb9","type":"tool_result","content":"1\t# Miroir — Implementation Plan\n2\t\n3\t**Multi-node Index Replication Orchestrator, Integrated Rebalancing**\n4\t\n5\tMiroir is a RAID-like sharding and high-availability layer for Meilisearch Community Edition. It stripes a large index across a fleet of Meilisearch nodes, fans out search queries across all shards, merges ranked results, and rebalances shard assignments when nodes are added or removed — all without Meilisearch Enterprise.\n6\t\n7\t---\n8\t\n9\t## Table of Contents\n10\t\n11\t1. [Design Principles](#1-design-principles)\n12\t2. [Architecture](#2-architecture)\n13\t3. [Document, Index, and Search Lifecycle](#3-document-index-and-search-lifecycle)\n14\t4. [Implementation](#4-implementation)\n15\t5. [API Surface and Compatibility](#5-api-surface-and-compatibility)\n16\t6. [Deployment](#6-deployment)\n17\t7. [CI/CD](#7-cicd)\n18\t8. [Testing](#8-testing)\n19\t9. [Secrets Handling](#9-secrets-handling)\n20\t10. [Observability](#10-observability)\n21\t11. [Onboarding](#11-onboarding)\n22\t12. [Delivered Artifacts](#12-delivered-artifacts)\n23\t13. [Advanced Capabilities](#13-advanced-capabilities)\n24\t14. [Resource Envelope and Horizontal Scaling](#14-resource-envelope-and-horizontal-scaling)\n25\t15. [Open Problems](#15-open-problems)\n26\t\n27\t---\n28\t\n29\t## 1. Design Principles\n30\t\n31\t1. **Invisible federation** — clients talk to one endpoint using the standard Meilisearch API. The sharding topology is entirely hidden. No SDK changes, no query changes, no schema changes.\n32\t2. **No Enterprise dependency** — all functionality is built on Meilisearch Community Edition (MIT licensed).\n33\t3. **Rendezvous hashing** — same algorithm Meilisearch Enterprise uses internally; minimal reshuffling on topology change, natural RF > 1 support.\n34\t4. **RF-configurable redundancy** — RF=1 for maximum capacity, RF=2 for one-node-loss tolerance, RF=3 for two-node-loss tolerance.\n35\t5. **Graceful degradation** — when a shard is unavailable, return partial results with a clear header rather than failing the entire request.\n36\t6. **Static binaries, scratch images** — musl compilation + scratch Docker base for minimal attack surface and trivial deployment.\n37\t7. **GitOps first** — all deployment configuration committed to `jedarden/declarative-config`; ArgoCD drives all cluster changes.\n38\t8. **Fixed per-pod resource envelope** — each Miroir orchestrator pod fits within **2 vCPU / 3.75 GB RAM**. When aggregate workload exceeds this envelope, scale **horizontally** by adding pods, never vertically beyond the envelope. The request path is strictly stateless; background work partitions across pods via shard-partitioned ownership, leader election, or a shared job queue. See Section 14.\n39\t\n40\t### Key constraints\n41\t\n42\t- **Logical shard count (S) is fixed at index creation** — this is the granularity of the hash space, not the number of physical machines. It determines how finely the keyspace is divided. Changing S requires a full reindex. Choose generously, per group: `S = max_nodes_per_group_ever × 8`. S is scoped to a single replica group because rendezvous assignment runs within each group independently (see Section 2); adding groups multiplies throughput without consuming additional S headroom.\n43\t- **Node count (N) is fully elastic** — nodes can be added or removed at any time without a full reindex. Adding a node to a group migrates only the `~1/(Ng+1)` fraction of that group's documents whose shard assignments change, where Ng is the number of nodes in the affected group. Documents in other groups are untouched. Removing a node migrates only that node's documents to surviving nodes within its own group. The rest of the corpus is untouched.\n44\t- All Meilisearch nodes must have **identical index settings** at all times. Miroir enforces this by broadcasting settings atomically.\n45\t- Documents **must** have an explicit primary key declared at index creation. Miroir cannot shard-route without it.\n46\t\n47\t---\n48\t\n49\t## 2. Architecture\n50\t\n51\t### Core model\n52\t\n53\tMiroir treats a fleet of Meilisearch CE instances the way software RAID treats a disk array, with an additional dimension for read throughput: **replica groups**.\n54\t\n55\t- The logical index is divided into **S shards** — a fixed hash-space granularity chosen at index creation\n56\t- The node fleet is divided into **RG replica groups** — independent pools each holding a complete copy of all shards\n57\t- Within each group, each shard is held by **RF nodes** (intra-group replication factor, for HA within the group)\n58\t- Every write fans out to all `RG × RF` target nodes (one per shard per group replica)\n59\t- Every search query is routed to exactly **one replica group** — the query fans out only to that group's covering set, not the entire fleet\n60\t- Read throughput scales with RG: doubling the groups doubles query capacity\n61\t- Storage capacity scales with total nodes: adding a node to a group reduces each node's share within that group\n62\t- The **node fleet is elastic**: nodes can be added to existing groups (capacity scaling) or new groups can be added (throughput scaling), both without a full reindex\n63\t- When the fleet topology changes, the orchestrator rebalances only the affected shards within the affected group\n64\t\n65\t```\n66\tClient\n67\t  │\n68\t  ▼\n69\tMiroir Orchestrator\n70\t  ├── Write path: hash(doc_id) → shard → fan out to RF nodes in EACH group (RG × RF total)\n71\t  ├── Read path:  pick one group → scatter to that group's covering set → merge results\n72\t  └── Rebalance: on node add/remove within a group → migrate minimum shards within that group\n73\t\n74\t  Replica Group 0              Replica Group 1\n75\t  ┌──────────────────┐        ┌──────────────────┐\n76\t  │ node-0  node-1   │        │ node-3  node-4   │     ...  (RG groups)\n77\t  │ node-2           │        │ node-5           │\n78\t  └──────────────────┘        └──────────────────┘\n79\t  (each group holds all S shards, distributed across its nodes)\n80\t```\n81\t\n82\t### Replication factor\n83\t\n84\t| RF | Redundancy | Node failures tolerated | Capacity |\n85\t|----|-----------|------------------------|----------|\n86\t| 1  | None (stripe only) | 0 | 100% of fleet |\n87\t| 2  | One replica | 1 per shard group | 50% of fleet |\n88\t| 3  | Two replicas | 2 per shard group | 33% of fleet |\n89\t\n90\t### Shard routing — Rendezvous hashing (HRW) within groups\n91\t\n92\tMiroir uses **Rendezvous hashing (HRW)** to assign shards to nodes. The assignment is scoped **within each replica group** — the rendezvous hash picks the top-RF nodes from a group's node list, not the global node list. This guarantees that every group independently forms a complete covering set with no cross-group shard overlap.\n93\t\n94\t```\n95\tnodes_in_group(g)           → the subset of nodes belonging to replica group g\n96\tassign_shard(shard_id, g)   → top RF nodes from nodes_in_group(g)\n97\t                              by score(hash(shard_id || node_id))\n98\t\n99\twrite_targets(shard_id)     → [assign_shard(shard_id, g) for g in 0..RG]\n100\t                              (flat union across all groups — RG × RF nodes total)"}]},"parent_tool_use_id":"call_8c3dc722974747cb963d581d","session_id":"a4129a13-6903-4406-9316-393d1af5e8b1","uuid":"bfa60e93-610f-443f-bdf5-089920f0e3ba","timestamp":"2026-05-09T16:10:03.733Z"}

{"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"call_a4122cc011c54a5498be3303","type":"tool_result","content":"1\t//! Shard migration cutover state machine.\n2\t//!\n3\t//! Implements the node-addition migration flow from plan §4 with explicit state\n4\t//! transitions and a race-window-safe cutover sequence.\n5\t//!\n6\t//! ## Race window analysis (plan §15 OP#1)\n7\t//!\n8\t//! The dangerous window is between \"mark node active\" (routing changes to new-node-only)\n9\t//! and \"delete migrated shard from old node.\" A document written during dual-write that\n10\t//! succeeded on OLD but failed on NEW — and arrived after the last migration page —\n11\t//! would be deleted from OLD without ever reaching NEW.\n12\t//!\n13\t//! ## Solution: quiesce-then-verify cutover\n14\t//!\n15\t//! Instead of the naïve sequence (mark active → stop dual-write → delete old), we use:\n16\t//!\n17\t//! 1. Stop dual-write (no new writes go to either node for affected shards)\n18\t//! 2. Drain: wait for all in-flight writes to both OLD and NEW to complete\n19\t//! 3. Delta migration: re-read affected shards from OLD (catches anything written since\n20\t//!    the last migration page) and write deltas to NEW\n21\t//! 4. Mark node active (routing switches to NEW-only)\n22\t//! 5. Delete migrated shard from OLD\n23\t//!\n24\t//! Step 3 is the key: it closes the race window by ensuring NEW has a complete picture\n25\t//! before we commit the routing change. The cost is one extra pagination pass over each\n26\t//! migrated shard — bounded by the number of docs written during the migration window.\n27\t\n28\tuse std::collections::{HashMap, HashSet};\n29\tuse std::fmt;\n30\tuse std::time::{Duration, Instant};\n31\t\n32\tuse serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};\n33\t\n34\t/// Unique identifier for a shard migration operation.\n35\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Hash, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n36\tpub struct MigrationId(pub u64);\n37\t\n38\timpl fmt::Display for MigrationId {\n39\t    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {\n40\t        write!(f, \"{}\", self.0)\n41\t    }\n42\t}\n43\t\n44\t/// Identifier for a physical node in the cluster.\n45\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n46\tpub struct NodeId(pub String);\n47\t\n48\timpl fmt::Display for NodeId {\n49\t    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {\n50\t        write!(f, \"{}\", self.0)\n51\t    }\n52\t}\n53\t\n54\t/// Identifier for a logical shard.\n55\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Hash, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n56\tpub struct ShardId(pub u32);\n57\t\n58\timpl fmt::Display for ShardId {\n59\t    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {\n60\t        write!(f, \"s{}\", self.0)\n61\t    }\n62\t}\n63\t\n64\t/// Per-shard migration state within a node-addition migration.\n65\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n66\tpub enum ShardMigrationState {\n67\t    /// Waiting for background migration to begin.\n68\t    Pending,\n69\t    /// Background pagination is reading docs from source and writing to target.\n70\t    Migrating {\n71\t        docs_copied: u64,\n72\t        pages_remaining: u32,\n73\t    },\n74\t    /// Background migration complete, awaiting cutover.\n75\t    MigrationComplete { docs_copied: u64 },\n76\t    /// Dual-write stopped, in-flight writes draining.\n77\t    Draining {\n78\t        in_flight_count: u32,\n79\t        docs_copied: u64,\n80\t    },\n81\t    /// Delta pass: re-reading source to catch stragglers written during migration.\n82\t    DeltaPass {\n83\t        docs_copied: u64,\n84\t        delta_docs_copied: u64,\n85\t    },\n86\t    /// Node is active for this shard; old replica data deleted.\n87\t    Active,\n88\t    /// Migration failed at this phase.\n89\t    Failed { phase: String, reason: String },\n90\t}\n91\t\n92\timpl fmt::Display for ShardMigrationState {\n93\t    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {\n94\t        match self {\n95\t            Self::Pending => write!(f, \"pending\"),\n96\t            Self::Migrating {\n97\t                docs_copied,\n98\t                pages_remaining,\n99\t            } => {\n100\t                write!(\n101\t                    f,\n102\t                    \"migrating({docs_copied} copied, {pages_remaining} pages left)\"\n103\t                )\n104\t            }\n105\t            Self::MigrationComplete { docs_copied } => {\n106\t                write!(f, \"migration_complete({docs_copied} copied)\")\n107\t            }\n108\t            Self::Draining {\n109\t                in_flight_count,\n110\t                docs_copied,\n111\t            } => {\n112\t                write!(\n113\t                    f,\n114\t                    \"draining({in_flight_count} in-flight, {docs_copied} copied)\"\n115\t                )\n116\t            }\n117\t            Self::DeltaPass {\n118\t                docs_copied,\n119\t                delta_docs_copied,\n120\t            } => {\n121\t                write!(f, \"delta_pass({docs_copied} + {delta_docs_copied} copied)\")\n122\t            }\n123\t            Self::Active => write!(f, \"active\"),\n124\t            Self::Failed { phase, reason } => write!(f, \"failed({phase}: {reason})\"),\n125\t        }\n126\t    }\n127\t}\n128\t\n129\t/// Overall migration phase for a node addition.\n130\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n131\tpub enum MigrationPhase {\n132\t    /// Computing which shards move to the new node.\n133\t    ComputingAssignments,\n134\t    /// Dual-write active; background migration in progress.\n135\t    DualWriteMigrating,\n136\t    /// Background migration done; beginning cutover.\n137\t    CutoverBegin,\n138\t    /// Stopping dual-write; waiting for in-flight writes to settle.\n139\t    CutoverDraining,\n140\t    /// Re-reading source to catch docs written during migration.\n141\t    CutoverDeltaPass,\n142\t    /// Marking new node active; switching routing.\n143\t    CutoverActivate,\n144\t    /// Deleting migrated shard data from old nodes.\n145\t    CutoverCleanup,\n146\t    /// All shards migrated; migration complete.\n147\t    Complete,\n148\t    /// Migration failed.\n149\t    Failed(String),\n150\t}\n151\t\n152\timpl fmt::Display for MigrationPhase {\n153\t    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {\n154\t        match self {\n155\t            Self::ComputingAssignments => write!(f, \"computing_assignments\"),\n156\t            Self::DualWriteMigrating => write!(f, \"dual_write_migrating\"),\n157\t            Self::CutoverBegin => write!(f, \"cutover_begin\"),\n158\t            Self::CutoverDraining => write!(f, \"cutover_draining\"),\n159\t            Self::CutoverDeltaPass => write!(f, \"cutover_delta_pass\"),\n160\t            Self::CutoverActivate => write!(f, \"cutover_activate\"),\n161\t            Self::CutoverCleanup => write!(f, \"cutover_cleanup\"),\n162\t            Self::Complete => write!(f, \"complete\"),\n163\t            Self::Failed(msg) => write!(f, \"failed({msg})\"),\n164\t        }\n165\t    }\n166\t}\n167\t\n168\t/// A single document write targeting a shard during migration.\n169\t#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\n170\tpub struct InFlightWrite {\n171\t    pub doc_id: String,\n172\t    pub shard: ShardId,\n173\t    pub target_nodes: Vec<NodeId>,\n174\t    pub completed_nodes: HashSet<NodeId>,\n175\t    pub failed_nodes: HashMap<NodeId, String>,\n176\t    pub submitted_at: Instant,\n177\t}\n178\t\n179\t// Serialize Instant as a placeholder bool (present/absent).\n180\t// Instant is monotonic and not meaningfully serializable across processes;\n181\t// on deserialize, reconstruct as Instant::now().\n182\tmod instant_serde {\n183\t    use serde::{Deserialize, Deserializer, Serialize, Serializer};\n184\t    use std::time::Instant;\n185\t\n186\t    pub fn serialize<S>(instant: &Option<Instant>, serializer: S) -> Result<S::Ok, S::Error>\n187\t    where\n188\t        S: Serializer,\n189\t    {\n190\t        instant.is_some().serialize(serializer)\n191\t    }\n192\t\n193\t    pub fn deserialize<'de, D>(deserializer: D) -> Result<Option<Instant>, D::Error>\n194\t    where\n195\t        D: Deserializer<'de>,\n196\t    {\n197\t        let present = bool::deserialize(deserializer)?;\n198\t        Ok(if present { Some(Instant::now()) } else { None })\n199\t    }\n200\t}\n201\t\n202\t/// Configuration for migration cutover behavior.\n203\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n204\tpub struct MigrationConfig {\n205\t    /// Maximum time to wait for in-flight writes to drain during cutover.\n206\t    pub drain_timeout: Duration,\n207\t    /// Whether to perform the delta pass (re-read source after stopping dual-write).\n208\t    /// Disabling this saves a pagination pass but opens the race window — only safe\n209\t    /// when anti-entropy is enabled as a safety net.\n210\t    pub skip_delta_pass: bool,\n211\t    /// Whether anti-entropy is enabled — used to determine if skip_delta_pass is safe.\n212\t    pub anti_entropy_enabled: bool,\n213\t}\n214\t\n215\timpl Default for MigrationConfig {\n216\t    fn default() -> Self {\n217\t        Self {\n218\t            drain_timeout: Duration::from_secs(30),\n219\t            skip_delta_pass: false,\n220\t            anti_entropy_enabled: true,\n221\t        }\n222\t    }\n223\t}\n224\t\n225\t/// Error type for migration operations.\n226\t#[derive(Debug, thiserror::Error)]\n227\tpub enum MigrationError {\n228\t    #[error(\n229\t        \"anti-entropy is disabled and delta pass is skipped — documents may be lost at cutover\"\n230\t    )]\n231\t    UnsafeCutoverNoAntiEntropy,\n232\t    #[error(\"drain timeout exceeded: {0} in-flight writes still pending\")]\n233\t    DrainTimeout(u32),\n234\t    #[error(\"shard {0} is not in a valid state for this transition (current: {1})\")]\n235\t    InvalidTransition(ShardId, String),\n236\t    #[error(\"migration {0} not found\")]\n237\t    NotFound(MigrationId),\n238\t    #[error(\"delta pass failed for shard {0}: {1}\")]\n239\t    DeltaPassFailed(ShardId, String),\n240\t}\n241\t\n242\t/// Tracks the state of a node-addition migration.\n243\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n244\tpub struct MigrationState {\n245\t    pub id: MigrationId,\n246\t    pub new_node: NodeId,\n247\t    pub replica_group: u32,\n248\t    pub phase: MigrationPhase,\n249\t    pub affected_shards: HashMap<ShardId, ShardMigrationState>,\n250\t    /// Maps shard → old node that currently owns it.\n251\t    pub old_owners: HashMap<ShardId, NodeId>,\n252\t    #[serde(with = \"instant_serde\")]\n253\t    pub started_at: Option<Instant>,\n254\t    #[serde(with = \"instant_serde\")]\n255\t    pub completed_at: Option<Instant>,\n256\t}\n257\t\n258\t/// The migration coordinator manages shard migration state transitions.\n259\tpub struct MigrationCoordinator {\n260\t    config: MigrationConfig,\n261\t    migrations: HashMap<MigrationId, MigrationState>,\n262\t    next_id: u64,\n263\t    /// In-flight writes being tracked for drain during cutover.\n264\t    in_flight: Vec<InFlightWrite>,\n265\t}\n266\t\n267\timpl MigrationCoordinator {\n268\t    pub fn new(config: MigrationConfig) -> Self {\n269\t        Self {\n270\t            config,\n271\t            migrations: HashMap::new(),\n272\t            next_id: 0,\n273\t            in_flight: Vec::new(),\n274\t        }\n275\t    }\n276\t\n277\t    /// Validate migration safety before starting. Returns an error if the configuration\n278\t    /// would allow data loss at the cutover boundary.\n279\t    pub fn validate_safety(&self) -> Result<(), MigrationError> {\n280\t        if self.config.skip_delta_pass && !self.config.anti_entropy_enabled {\n281\t            return Err(MigrationError::UnsafeCutoverNoAntiEntropy);\n282\t        }\n283\t        Ok(())\n284\t    }\n285\t\n286\t    /// Begin a new node-addition migration.\n287\t    pub fn begin_migration(\n288\t        &mut self,\n289\t        new_node: NodeId,\n290\t        replica_group: u32,\n291\t        affected_shards: HashMap<ShardId, NodeId>,\n292\t    ) -> Result<MigrationId, MigrationError> {\n293\t        self.validate_safety()?;\n294\t\n295\t        let id = MigrationId(self.next_id);\n296\t        self.next_id += 1;\n297\t\n298\t        let shard_states: HashMap<ShardId, ShardMigrationState> = affected_shards\n299\t            .keys()\n300\t            .map(|&shard| (shard, ShardMigrationState::Pending))\n301\t            .collect();\n302\t\n303\t        let state = MigrationState {\n304\t            id,\n305\t            new_node,\n306\t            replica_group,\n307\t            phase: MigrationPhase::ComputingAssignments,\n308\t            affected_shards: shard_states,\n309\t            old_owners: affected_shards,\n310\t            started_at: Some(Instant::now()),\n311\t            completed_at: None,\n312\t        };\n313\t\n314\t        self.migrations.insert(id, state);\n315\t        Ok(id)\n316\t    }\n317\t\n318\t    /// Transition to dual-write + background migration phase.\n319\t    pub fn begin_dual_write(&mut self, id: MigrationId) -> Result<(), MigrationError> {\n320\t        let state = self\n321\t            .migrations\n322\t            .get_mut(&id)\n323\t            .ok_or(MigrationError::NotFound(id))?;\n324\t        state.phase = MigrationPhase::DualWriteMigrating;\n325\t        for shard_state in state.affected_shards.values_mut() {\n326\t            if *shard_state == ShardMigrationState::Pending {\n327\t                *shard_state = ShardMigrationState::Migrating {\n328\t                    docs_copied: 0,\n329\t                    pages_remaining: 0,\n330\t                };\n331\t            }\n332\t        }\n333\t        Ok(())\n334\t    }\n335\t\n336\t    /// Record that a shard's background migration completed.\n337\t    pub fn shard_migration_complete(\n338\t        &mut self,\n339\t        id: MigrationId,\n340\t        shard: ShardId,\n341\t        docs_copied: u64,\n342\t    ) -> Result<(), MigrationError> {\n343\t        let state = self\n344\t            .migrations\n345\t            .get_mut(&id)\n346\t            .ok_or(MigrationError::NotFound(id))?;\n347\t        let shard_state = state.affected_shards.get_mut(&shard).ok_or_else(|| {\n348\t            MigrationError::InvalidTransition(shard, \"shard not in migration\".into())\n349\t        })?;\n350\t\n351\t        match shard_state {\n352\t            ShardMigrationState::Migrating { .. } => {\n353\t                *shard_state = ShardMigrationState::MigrationComplete { docs_copied };\n354\t            }\n355\t            _ => {\n356\t                return Err(MigrationError::InvalidTransition(\n357\t                    shard,\n358\t                    shard_state.to_string(),\n359\t                ));\n360\t            }\n361\t        }\n362\t\n363\t        // Check if all shards are done migrating\n364\t        let all_complete = state\n365\t            .affected_shards\n366\t            .values()\n367\t            .all(|s| matches!(s, ShardMigrationState::MigrationComplete { .. }));\n368\t\n369\t        if all_complete {\n370\t            state.phase = MigrationPhase::CutoverBegin;\n371\t        }\n372\t\n373\t        Ok(())\n374\t    }\n375\t\n376\t    /// Begin the cutover sequence: stop dual-write and drain in-flight writes.\n377\t    pub fn begin_cutover(&mut self, id: MigrationId) -> Result<MigrationPhase, MigrationError> {\n378\t        let state = self\n379\t            .migrations\n380\t            .get_mut(&id)\n381\t            .ok_or(MigrationError::NotFound(id))?;\n382\t\n383\t        if !matches!(state.phase, MigrationPhase::CutoverBegin) {\n384\t            return Err(MigrationError::InvalidTransition(\n385\t                ShardId(0),\n386\t                format!(\"expected CutoverBegin, got {}\", state.phase),\n387\t            ));\n388\t        }\n389\t\n390\t        // Transition all shards to Draining\n391\t        let total_in_flight = self.in_flight.len() as u32;\n392\t        for (shard, shard_state) in state.affected_shards.iter_mut() {\n393\t            match shard_state {\n394\t                ShardMigrationState::MigrationComplete { docs_copied } => {\n395\t                    *shard_state = ShardMigrationState::Draining {\n396\t                        in_flight_count: total_in_flight,\n397\t                        docs_copied: *docs_copied,\n398\t                    };\n399\t                }\n400\t                _ => {\n401\t                    return Err(MigrationError::InvalidTransition(\n402\t                        *shard,\n403\t                        shard_state.to_string(),\n404\t                    ));\n405\t                }\n406\t            }\n407\t        }\n408\t\n409\t        state.phase = MigrationPhase::CutoverDraining;\n410\t        Ok(state.phase.clone())\n411\t    }\n412\t\n413\t    /// Register an in-flight write for tracking during drain.\n414\t    pub fn register_in_flight(&mut self, write: InFlightWrite) {\n415\t        self.in_flight.push(write);\n416\t    }\n417\t\n418\t    /// Acknowledge completion of a write to a specific node.\n419\t    pub fn ack_write(&mut self, doc_id: &str, node: &NodeId) {\n420\t        for write in &mut self.in_flight {\n421\t            if write.doc_id == doc_id {\n422\t                write.completed_nodes.insert(node.clone());\n423\t            }\n424\t        }\n425\t    }\n426\t\n427\t    /// Mark a write as failed on a specific node.\n428\t    pub fn fail_write(&mut self, doc_id: &str, node: &NodeId, reason: String) {\n429\t        for write in &mut self.in_flight {\n430\t            if write.doc_id == doc_id {\n431\t                write.failed_nodes.insert(node.clone(), reason.clone());\n432\t            }\n433\t        }\n434\t    }\n435\t\n436\t    /// Check if all in-flight writes have completed (drained).\n437\t    pub fn is_drained(&self) -> bool {\n438\t        self.in_flight\n439\t            .iter()\n440\t            .all(|w| w.completed_nodes.len() + w.failed_nodes.len() == w.target_nodes.len())\n441\t    }\n442\t\n443\t    /// Complete the drain and move to delta pass or activation.\n444\t    pub fn complete_drain(&mut self, id: MigrationId) -> Result<MigrationPhase, MigrationError> {\n445\t        // First check phase exists without holding mutable borrow\n446\t        let phase = self\n447\t            .migrations\n448\t            .get(&id)\n449\t            .ok_or(MigrationError::NotFound(id))?\n450\t            .phase\n451\t            .clone();\n452\t\n453\t        if !matches!(phase, MigrationPhase::CutoverDraining) {\n454\t            return Err(MigrationError::InvalidTransition(\n455\t                ShardId(0),\n456\t                format!(\"expected CutoverDraining, got {phase}\"),\n457\t            ));\n458\t        }\n459\t\n460\t        // Check drain status\n461\t        if !self.is_drained() {\n462\t            let remaining = self\n463\t                .in_flight\n464\t                .iter()\n465\t                .filter(|w| w.completed_nodes.len() + w.failed_nodes.len() < w.target_nodes.len())\n466\t                .count() as u32;\n467\t            return Err(MigrationError::DrainTimeout(remaining));\n468\t        }\n469\t\n470\t        // Collect docs that need delta pass\n471\t        let needs_delta = self.collect_delta_candidates(id)?;\n472\t        let skip_delta = self.config.skip_delta_pass;\n473\t\n474\t        // Now get mutable borrow to update state\n475\t        let state = self\n476\t            .migrations\n477\t            .get_mut(&id)\n478\t            .ok_or(MigrationError::NotFound(id))?;\n479\t\n480\t        if skip_delta {\n481\t            // Skip delta pass — safe only if anti-entropy is enabled\n482\t            state.phase = MigrationPhase::CutoverActivate;\n483\t        } else if needs_delta.is_empty() {\n484\t            state.phase = MigrationPhase::CutoverActivate;\n485\t        } else {\n486\t            state.phase = MigrationPhase::CutoverDeltaPass;\n487\t            for (_shard, shard_state) in state.affected_shards.iter_mut() {\n488\t                if let ShardMigrationState::Draining { docs_copied, .. } = shard_state {\n489\t                    *shard_state = ShardMigrationState::DeltaPass {\n490\t                        docs_copied: *docs_copied,\n491\t                        delta_docs_copied: 0,\n492\t                    };\n493\t                }\n494\t            }\n495\t        }\n496\t\n497\t        // Clear only the in-flight writes for this migration\n498\t        let affected_shards = state\n499\t            .affected_shards\n500\t            .keys()\n501\t            .cloned()\n502\t            .collect::<HashSet<_>>();\n503\t        self.in_flight\n504\t            .retain(|w| !affected_shards.contains(&w.shard));\n505\t\n506\t        // If going to activate, do that now (drop mutable borrow first)\n507\t        let next_phase = state.phase.clone();\n508\t        if matches!(next_phase, MigrationPhase::CutoverActivate) {\n509\t            let _ = state;\n510\t            self.activate_shards(id)?;\n511\t            // Return the new phase after activation\n512\t            return Ok(self\n513\t                .migrations\n514\t                .get(&id)\n515\t                .map(|s| s.phase.clone())\n516\t                .unwrap_or(MigrationPhase::CutoverCleanup));\n517\t        }\n518\t\n519\t        Ok(next_phase)\n520\t    }\n521\t\n522\t    /// Identify writes that need the delta pass — those that succeeded on OLD but\n523\t    /// failed (or never reached) NEW.\n524\t    fn collect_delta_candidates(\n525\t        &self,\n526\t        id: MigrationId,\n527\t    ) -> Result<HashMap<ShardId, Vec<String>>, MigrationError> {\n528\t        let state = self\n529\t            .migrations\n530\t            .get(&id)\n531\t            .ok_or(MigrationError::NotFound(id))?;\n532\t        let mut candidates: HashMap<ShardId, Vec<String>> = HashMap::new();\n533\t\n534\t        for write in &self.in_flight {\n535\t            let old_owner = match state.old_owners.get(&write.shard) {\n536\t                Some(owner) => owner,\n537\t                None => continue,\n538\t            };\n539\t\n540\t            let succeeded_on_old = write.completed_nodes.contains(old_owner);\n541\t            let succeeded_on_new = write.completed_nodes.contains(&state.new_node);\n542\t\n543\t            // Doc is on OLD but not on NEW — delta pass must catch it\n544\t            if succeeded_on_old && !succeeded_on_new {\n545\t                candidates\n546\t                    .entry(write.shard)\n547\t                    .or_default()\n548\t                    .push(write.doc_id.clone());\n549\t            }\n550\t        }\n551\t\n552\t        Ok(candidates)\n553\t    }\n554\t\n555\t    /// Record that the delta pass completed for a shard.\n556\t    pub fn shard_delta_complete(\n557\t        &mut self,\n558\t        id: MigrationId,\n559\t        shard: ShardId,\n560\t        delta_docs: u64,\n561\t    ) -> Result<(), MigrationError> {\n562\t        let state = self\n563\t            .migrations\n564\t            .get_mut(&id)\n565\t            .ok_or(MigrationError::NotFound(id))?;\n566\t        let shard_state = state.affected_shards.get_mut(&shard).ok_or_else(|| {\n567\t            MigrationError::InvalidTransition(shard, \"shard not in migration\".into())\n568\t        })?;\n569\t\n570\t        match shard_state {\n571\t            ShardMigrationState::DeltaPass { docs_copied, .. } => {\n572\t                *shard_state = ShardMigrationState::MigrationComplete {\n573\t                    docs_copied: *docs_copied + delta_docs,\n574\t                };\n575\t            }\n576\t            _ => {\n577\t                return Err(MigrationError::InvalidTransition(\n578\t                    shard,\n579\t                    shard_state.to_string(),\n580\t                ));\n581\t            }\n582\t        }\n583\t\n584\t        // Check if all shards done with delta\n585\t        let all_complete = state\n586\t            .affected_shards\n587\t            .values()\n588\t            .all(|s| matches!(s, ShardMigrationState::MigrationComplete { .. }));\n589\t\n590\t        if all_complete {\n591\t            state.phase = MigrationPhase::CutoverActivate;\n592\t            self.activate_shards(id)?;\n593\t        }\n594\t\n595\t        Ok(())\n596\t    }\n597\t\n598\t    /// Mark all affected shards as active on the new node.\n599\t    fn activate_shards(&mut self, id: MigrationId) -> Result<(), MigrationError> {\n600\t        let state = self\n601\t            .migrations\n602\t            .get_mut(&id)\n603\t            .ok_or(MigrationError::NotFound(id))?;\n604\t\n605\t        for shard_state in state.affected_shards.values_mut() {\n606\t            match shard_state {\n607\t                ShardMigrationState::MigrationComplete { .. }\n608\t                | ShardMigrationState::Draining { .. } => {\n609\t                    *shard_state = ShardMigrationState::Active;\n610\t                }\n611\t                _ => {}\n612\t            }\n613\t        }\n614\t\n615\t        if matches!(state.phase, MigrationPhase::CutoverActivate) {\n616\t            state.phase = MigrationPhase::CutoverCleanup;\n617\t        }\n618\t\n619\t        Ok(())\n620\t    }\n621\t\n622\t    /// Complete the migration by deleting migrated shard data from old nodes.\n623\t    pub fn complete_cleanup(&mut self, id: MigrationId) -> Result<(), MigrationError> {\n624\t        let state = self\n625\t            .migrations\n626\t            .get_mut(&id)\n627\t            .ok_or(MigrationError::NotFound(id))?;\n628\t\n629\t        if !matches!(state.phase, MigrationPhase::CutoverCleanup) {\n630\t            return Err(MigrationError::InvalidTransition(\n631\t                ShardId(0),\n632\t                format!(\"expected CutoverCleanup, got {}\", state.phase),\n633\t            ));\n634\t        }\n635\t\n636\t        state.phase = MigrationPhase::Complete;\n637\t        state.completed_at = Some(Instant::now());\n638\t        Ok(())\n639\t    }\n640\t\n641\t    /// Get the current state of a migration.\n642\t    pub fn (deterministic JSON output).\n70\tpub fn merge(input: MergeInput) -> MergedSearchResult {\n71\t    // Filter to only successful responses\n72\t    let successful_shards: Vec<_> = input\n73\t        .shard_hits\n74\t        .iter()\n75\t        .filter(|s| s.success)\n76\t        .collect();\n77\t\n78\t    // Check if any shards failed (degraded mode)\n79\t    let degraded =                   .get(\"_rankingScore\")\n89\t                    .and_then(|s| s.as_f64())\n90\t                    .unwrap_or(0.0);\n91\t\n92\t                let primary_key = hit\n93\t        // Reverse<T> makes the \"smallest\" T become the \"largest\" Reverse<T>\n113\t        // So in BinaryHeap (max-heap), the smallest T ends up at the top\n114\t        use std::cmp::Reverse;\n115\t\n116\t        // First, define a wrapper with natural ascending order by score\n117\t        #[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq)]\n118\t        struct AscendingHit(HitWithScore);\n119\t\n120\t        impl PartialOrd for AscendingHit {\n121\t            fn partial_cmp(&self, other: &Self) -> Option<std::cmp::Ordering> {\n122\t                Some(self.cmp(other))\n123\t            }\n124\t        }\n125\t\n126\t        impl Ord for AscendingHit {\n127\t            fn cmp(&self, other: &Self) -> std::cmp::Ordering {\n128\t                // Ascending order: lower score first, then primary key ascending\n129\t                match self.0.score.partial_cmp(&other.0.score) {\n130\t                    Some(std::cmp::Ordering::Equal) | None => {\n131\t                        self.0.primary_key.cmp(&other.0.primary_key)\n132\t                    }\n133\t                    Some(ord) => ord,\n134\t                }\n135\t            }\n136\t        }\n137\t\n138\t        // Reverse<AscendingHit> in BinaryHeap gives us a min-heap by score\n139\t        // The lowest score (worst) will be at the top for easy replacement\n140\t heap.push(Reverse(AscendingHit(hit)));\n145\t            } else {\n146\t                // Peek at the smallest (worst) hit in our top-k\n147\t                if let Some(Reverse(worst)) = heap.peek() {\n148\t                    // If current hit is better than our worst, replace it\n149\t                    // Compare using the score directly\n150\t                    if hit.score > worst.0.score ||\n151\t                       (hit.score == worst.0.score && hit.primary_key < worst.0.primary_key) {\n152\t                        heap.pop();\n153\t                        heap.push(Reverse(AscendingHit(hit)));\n154\t                    }\n155\t                }\n156\t            }\n157\t        }\n158\t\n159\t        // Convert to sorted vector (descending by   // For smaller result sets, just sort directly\n165\t        all_hits.sort_by(|a, b| a.descending_cmp(b));\n166\t        all_hits\n167\t    };\n168\t\n169\t    // Apply offset and limit\n170\t }\n238\t}\n239\t\n240\timpl HitWithScore {\n241\t    /// Compare for descending order (score desc, primary key asc).\n242\t    fn descending_cmp(&self, other: &Self) -> std::cmp::Ordering {\n243\t        // Sort by score descending, then by primary key ascending for tie-breaking\n244\t        match other.score.partial_cmp(&self.score) {\n245\t            Some(std::cmp::Ordering::Equal) | None => {\n246\t                // On equal scores (or NaN), fall back to primary key ascending\n247\t                self.primary_key.cmp(&other.primary_key)\n248\t            }\n249\t            Some(ord) .collect();\n404\t\n405\t    Value::Object(result)\n406\t}\n407\t\n408\t/// Stub implementation that returns empty results.\n409\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, Default)]\n410\tpub struct NodeStatus {\n55\t    /// Check if a transition from `self` to `new_status` is valid.\n56\t    ///\n57\t    /// # State Transition Rules\n58\t    ///\n59\t    /// | From | To | Triggered by |\n60\t    /// |------|-----|-------------|\n61\t    /// | (new) | Joining | `POST /_miroir/nodes` |\n62\t    /// | Joining | Active | Migration complete |\n63\t    /// | Active | Draining | `POST /_miroir/nodes/{id}/drain` |\n64\t    /// | Draining | Removed | Migration complete |\n65\t    /// | Active/Draining | Failed | Health check detects |\n66\t    /// | Failed | Active | Health check {\n70\t        match (self, new_status) {\n71\t            // Initial state\n72\t            (NodeStatus::Joining, NodeStatus::Active) => true,\n73\t\n74\t            // Normal operations\n75\t            (NodeStatus::Active, NodeStatus::Draining) => true,\n76\t            (NodeStatus::Draining, NodeStatus::Removed) => true,\n77\t\n78\t            // Failure and recovery\n79\t            (NodeStatus::Active, NodeStatus::Failed) => true,\n80\t            (NodeStatus::Draining, NodeStatus::Failed) => true,\n81\t            (NodeStatus::Failed, NodeStatus::Active) => true,\n82\t\n83\t            // Degradation\n84\t            (NodeStatus::Active, NodeStatus::Degraded) => true,\n85\t            (NodeStatus::Failed, NodeStatus::Degraded) => true,\n86\t            (NodeStatus::Degraded, NodeStatus::Active) => true,\n87\t\n88\t            // Healthy <-> Active are bidirectional (synonyms)\n89\t            (NodeStatus::Healthy, NodeStatus::Active) => true,\n90\t            (NodeStatus::Active, NodeStatus::Healthy) => true,\n91\t\n92\t            // Same state is always valid\n93\t            (s, t) if s == t => true,\n94\t\n95\t            // All other transitions are invalid\n96\t            _ => false,\n97\t        }\n98\t    }\n99\t\n100\t    /// Returns `true` if the node can accept writes for the given shard.\n101\t    ///\n102\t    /// # Write Eligibility |--------|----------------|-------|\n108\t    /// | Healthy/Active | Yes | Normal operation |\n109\t    /// | Degraded | Yes | Partial failures, still accepting writes |\n110\t    /// | Joining | No | is_write_eligible_for(self, draining_shard: Option<u32>) -> bool {\n120\t        match self {\n121\t            NodeStatus::Healthy | NodeStatus::Active | NodeStatus::Degraded => true,\n122\t            NodeStatus::Joining | NodeStatus::Failed | NodeStatus::Removed => false,\n123\t            NodeStatus::Draining => !draining_shard.is_some(),\n124\t        }\n125\t    }\n126\t}\n127\t\n128\timpl fmt::Display for NodeStatus {\n129\t    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {\n130\t        match self {\n131\t            NodeStatus::Healthy => write!(f, \"healthy\"),\n132\t            NodeStatus::Degraded => write!(f, \"degraded\"),\n133\t            NodeStatus::Active => write!(f, \"active\"),\n134\t            NodeStatus::Joining => write!(f, \"joining\"),\n135\t            NodeStatus::Draining => write!(f, \"draining\"),\n136\t            NodeStatus::Failed => write!(f, \"failed\"),\n137\t            NodeStatus::Removed => write!(f, \"removed\"),\n138\t        }\n139\t    }\n140\t}\n141\t\n142\t/// A single Meilisearch node in the topology.\n143\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n144\tpub struct Node {\n145\t    /// Unique node replica_group,\n166\t        }\n167\t    }\n168\t\n169\t    /// Create a new node with a specific status.\n170\t    pub fn with_status(id: NodeId, address: String, replica_group: u32, status:  /// Transition the node to a new status, validating the transition.\n185\t    ///\n186\t    /// Returns `Ok(())` if the transition is valid, `Err` otherwise.\n187\t    pub fn set_status(&mut self, new_status: NodeStatus) -> Result<(), TransitionError> {\n188\t        if self.status.can_transition_to(new_status) {\n189\t            self.status = new_status;\n190\t            Ok(())\n191\t        } else {\n192\t            Err(TransitionError {\n193\t                from: self.status,\n194\t                to: new_status,\n195\t            })\n196\t        }\n197\t    }\n198\t\n199\t    ///
